[2023-03-23 01:03:40] => OpenAI Response => 

WarThunder is a free-to-play multiplayer online combat flight simulator video game developed and published by Gaijin Entertainment. WarThunder was first released on June 19, 2018, and is available on Windows, Mac, PlayStation 4, PlayStation 5, Xbox One, Xbox Series X/S, and Linux platforms. The game features various aerial, ground, and naval combat vehicles from the 1930s through the Cold War period.

Players can take control of planes from countries like Germany, Britain, America, and Japan to engage in dogfighting missions or engage in ground battles using tanks and armored vehicles. WarThunder has three playable modes - Arcade mode, Realistic mode, and Simulator mode. In Arcade mode, novice pilots can familiarize themselves with the game's mechanics while more experienced players can pit their skills against seasoned veterans in the more challenging Simulator mode.

Apart from the standard gameplay modes, WarThunder features co-operative missions, tournaments, and custom battles. Players can also earn in-game currency to upgrade their planes or purchase new vehicles. With the addition of new vehicles and features, War Thunder has become one of the most popular multiplayer combat games, providing players with hours of exciting gameplay.
